 How to get money on Mercury Pradosh- Great boon of money - On the day of Mercury Pradosh, elders of the house donate sweets and green items to the needy children from the hands of their children
 - pradosh vrath ke din 5 supaari / 5 ilaychi or paanch modak bhagwaan ganesh ko arpit karen
 - Light a lamp of ghee in front of Lord Ganesha and do a garland of chanting 'gan Ganpataye Namah Mantra' while sitting on the pedestal
